<script>
$(document).ready(function(){
    var url = new URL(window.location); // Construct URL object using current browser URL
    var params = url.searchParams; // Get query parameters object
    var S4Kcentre = params.get("S4Kcentre"); // Get value of S4Kcentre
    $("#S4Kcentre").val(S4Kcentre); // Set it as the dropdown value
    $("select").change(function(){
        $(this).find("option:selected").each(function(){
            var optionValue = $(this).attr("value");
            window.history.pushState(null, null, "?S4Kcentre=" + optionValue);
            if(optionValue){
                $(".centre").not("." + optionValue).hide();
                $("." + optionValue).show();
            }
        });
    }).change();
});

<p>Thank you to every single teacher at S4K Campus @ Yishun. Kudos to everyone of you who have taught and cared for O***** ever since Infant care, PG, N1 and N2 now. Especially during this challenging time with HBL during circuit breaker or school closures due to the Pandemic. When lessons are back in school, you have to think hard on how to make lessons fun for kids while keeping them safe through this pandemic. It must be hard wearing a mask all day in non air-conditioned classrooms, and having to keep these little monkeys disciplined and having them follow instructions while wearing a mask. These past few years haven’t been easy for everyone. It wasn’t just about Covid, as there were also HFMD, Stomach flu and common colds all year round. A teacher not only needs to teach them the normal syllabus but also need to educate the young kids what are viruses and how to be hygienic. It must be also tough to let such young kids learn how to keep the mask on and maintain a safe social distance from one another. Having said all of that, I only have full admiration and respect for all his teachers and the assistant teachers who have cared for him everyday, especially Teacher Y**** and A* Laoshi! They have taught my elder girl very well though her preschool years previously, and now teaching O***** too. I never had to worry about their learning when they are in your hands. 尤其是*老师, 自从你开始教**华文，他对华文的兴趣加深了很多，谢谢你！有你教他，真好！</p>
<p>THANK YOU and THANK YOU and THANK YOU from the bottom of my heart.</p>
